Important Foreign Telegrams

Britain Implements Austerity and Tax Increases

Emergency Budget Submitted to the House of Commons

The National Atmosphere Suddenly Becomes Tense

The Government Adopts Extraordinary Measures to Deal with the Special Environment

The Deficit Can Still Be Offset with a Surplus of £1.5 Million

▲Reuters, London, 10th: The government's austerity plan was announced tonight. According to the plan, the government can immediately implement various austerity measures that have been proposed. The plan authorizes the British monarch to issue privy council orders deemed necessary within one month of the plan's implementation to implement austerity measures in public undertakings. The administrative events specifically mentioned in the plan, which are applicable to the privy council order, are education, national health, insurance, police, unemployment insurance, and roads. The privy council's orders do not require parliamentary approval and become law once promulgated. This procedure is rarely used in Britain and is only adopted in special circumstances. In the current situation, this procedure can be considered necessary for the sake of expediency. If a motion is submitted according to ordinary government procedures, it will inevitably be delayed and leave room for obstruction.

▲Reuters, London, 11th: It is not yet certain whether there will be a reaction to the active austerity and sacrifice program announced by Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden yesterday when he submitted the emergency budget to the House of Commons. However, the tense atmosphere that existed in the House of Commons before the budget was submitted seemed to have eased last night. In the evening, various newspapers issued special editions outside the Parliament to disseminate the Ministry of Finance's plan to the public. Almost everyone in the country is now talking about the budget measures. The increase in the standard rate of income tax and the reduction of various exemptions will greatly affect a large portion of the population. Those who previously had little income and were exempt from tax will now have an obligation to pay taxes. Among those who currently pay income tax, those in the middle class who rely on salaries and professions for a living will be most affected. However, the people now seem to be completely determined to make major sacrifices, and resignation has become the current buzzword.

Scene in the Parliament

The House of Commons was extremely crowded in the afternoon, which was rare in the past. When Snowden arrived at the House of Commons, the crowd cheered thunderously. When he entered the arena, the government faction also cheered to welcome him. Snowden rose to speak, first declaring that he would carry out the most unpleasant work he had never done in his life, and then began his program to make up for the national deficit. Mr. Snowden's budget speech this time was truly the most astonishing budget speech ever made in Britain.

Summary of Figures

The figures involved in the new budget plan can be summarized as follows: Snowden not only spoke about the position of income within the remaining number in this fiscal year, but also about the position in the next fiscal year. It is estimated that the budget for this year is short of £74,000,000, the reason being the world's industrial depression and reduced tax revenue. Domestic tax revenue is £65,000,000 less than the budget, customs and domestic tax revenue is £4,000,000 less, and the revenue from the UK's war debts under President Hoover's suspension plan is also reduced by £30,000,000. Snowden proposes to make up for the above shortages by: austerity £22,000,000, less provision for debt repayment £13,700,000, tax increases £40,000,000, totaling £76,200,000. In this way, the shortage of £74 million can be turned into a surplus of £1.5 million. As for the next fiscal year, according to the current expenditure and income, there will be a shortage of £170,000,000. To make up for this, the measures are as follows: austerity £70,000,000, less provision for debt repayment £20,000,000, tax increases £81,500,000, totaling £171,500,000.

Details of Austerity

The government has issued a white paper containing details of the austerity measures in the budget, with the aim of saving a total of £70,000,000 in national expenditure throughout the year. The most politically contentious of these measures is the change in the basis of unemployment insurance benefits, which alone can save £25,800,000 per year. The savings in education expenditure, including a 15% reduction in teachers' salaries, can amount to £10,300,000. Unemployment benefits will be reduced by 10%, and unemployment benefits will be limited to six weeks, after which they must be tested, otherwise they will not be able to receive benefits again. After this, the measure of borrowing to pay for unemployment benefits will be stopped. Other austerity measures, such as salary cuts for cabinet members, parliamentarians, soldiers, civilians, and officials, will amount to £4,500,000. Cabinet members with salaries of £5,000 per year will have their salaries reduced by 20%, and parliamentarians with annual salaries of £400 will have their salaries reduced by 10%. Judges' salaries will also be reduced accordingly. The pay of soldiers in the national defense forces will be paid according to the pay scale of those who enlisted after 1925. Officers' salaries will also be reduced to a level commensurate with the cost of living. In addition, military spending is planned to be reduced further, for a total saving of £5,000,000. Police expenditure can also be saved by £500,000. Road expenditure will be saved by approximately £7,800,000. Colonial development expenditure will be limited to £750,000 next year, saving £250,000. The British Empire Marketing Board's expenditure will also be cut by £250,000.

Collection of New Taxes

It is estimated that tax revenue will need to be increased by £81,500,000 in the next fiscal year. The measures are as follows: the standard rate of income tax is currently 4 shillings and 6 pence per pound, and will be 5 shillings in the future. However, businesses will be compensated separately, that is, the existing exemption for depreciation of fixed assets will be increased to offset the increase in income tax. In addition, income tax exemptions and special reductions will be strictly eliminated. Unmarried persons with an annual income of less than £135 were previously exempt from tax, but this is no longer the case. Only those with an annual income of less than £100 will be exempt from tax. The tax exemption limit for married persons was previously an annual income of £225, but it has now been reduced to £150. The annual allowance for children, previously £60 for the first child, is now £50, and the allowance for the remaining children has been reduced from £50 to £40. Income tax is more favorable for labor-earned income. Previously, one-sixth of labor-earned wages were exempt from income tax, up to a limit of £250. This has now been changed to one-fifth exempt from tax, up to a limit of £300. The surtax will be increased by 10%. In terms of indirect taxes, the tax on beer will be increased by one penny per pint, the tax on imported tobacco was previously 8 shillings and 10 pence per pound, but will now be 9 shillings and 6 pence. Other tobacco will be taxed accordingly. The tax on oil will be increased by two pennies per gallon, and entertainment tax will be levied according to the new regulations, even on cheap seats. The maximum tax will be two pennies, but children's tickets will not be taxed.

Newspaper Criticism

Snowden's budget will naturally be criticized by the Labor Party. The measures he has proposed will inevitably face extremely fierce opposition in the legislative process. This morning, the Labor Party's mouthpiece, the Daily Herald, launched a major attack, saying that the sacrifices of the rich and the poor are not equal, and that Snowden has changed the course of his life's work and is going against the tide under pressure from the Conservative Party, the Liberal Party, and the bankers. The Conservative and Liberal Party newspapers said that they are capable of distributing and averaging the burden. The rich and the poor will show the world an honorable solution with one heart. Even if there is harm, they can only accept it. Otherwise, the panic would not be limited to this. The measures are indeed harsh, but in the circumstances of the previous month, Snowden had no other choice. Such were the detailed discussions in the newspapers. Last night, after the budget was submitted, a member of the House of Commons said to a Reuters reporter, "Let's have a drink while the price is up." The spirit of the people accepting this severe plan can be seen from these words. The Conservative Party is also alarmed by the heavy burden of income tax. Take the example of a family with two children whose annual salary is £500. They previously paid £8 in income tax, but will now have to pay £60.

Plan to Exchange Bonds

The Finance Bill contains a proposal to allow the government to exchange 5% war bonds for lower-interest bonds. Snowden mentioned this in his budget speech, saying that since 1929, the situation has been unstable, so this plan has not been implemented. He intends to ask Parliament to authorize the government to formulate a plan to ask those who hold 5% war bonds to exchange them for new bonds. If the bondholders do not object within three months of the issuance of the exchange notice, it will be deemed that they have agreed. In order to implement this plan, the government is requested to grant this power so that the Ministry of Finance can formulate measures to change the interest rate and extend the repayment period. This kind of exchange is unprecedented in world history and will require a considerable period of time to carry out. It will take several months to complete.

Waiting for its price to rise. The spirit of the people accepting this severe plan can be seen from this saying. The Conservative Party is also alarmed because the burden of income tax is very heavy. To try with a family with two children, the person who earns an annual salary of 500 pounds, from now on will have to pay 60 pounds.

Plan for Bond Exchange

The Financial Law contains a proposal to allow the government to exchange five-li war bonds for lower interest rate bonds. Snowden mentioned this in his budget speech and said that the situation had been uncertain since 1929, so this plan had not been implemented. The official plans to ask Congress to authorize the government to formulate a plan, requesting those holding five-li war bonds to exchange them for new coupons. If the holders of the coupon have no objection within three months of the issuance of the exchange notice, it shall be deemed that they have agreed to implement this plan, and requesting Congress to authorize this power, the Ministry of Finance may formulate methods to change the interest rate and extend the repayment period. This type of exchange is unprecedented in world history and needs a considerable period of time to carry out. It takes months to complete.

Opposition's Attack

After Snowden spoke for an hour and seventeen minutes and sat down, his supporters cheered for a long time. Former Secretary of Commerce Graham stood up and said that if the provision for debt repayment reserve funds were completely omitted, it could temporarily cope with the current financial situation. The government's proposed measures are inconsistent with the principle of equal sacrifice. People in the labor sector without any guarantees would be the only ones to suffer. The Labor Party cannot agree to this. The Labor Party then proposed a motion to reject the national austerity plan, signed by four former cabinet members including Klein, stating that the House recognizes the need to maintain national finances on a sound basis but cannot accept a plan that deprives the majority of the people of their basic necessities while allowing others to live in luxury. This plan would limit the purchasing power of workers, further increasing unemployment. The national austerity plan seeks to replace existing laws with orders from the Privy Council or to change national policies abruptly without the consent of the House. The Labor Party cannot agree to this. This afternoon, the Prime Minister will propose the second reading of the austerity plan.

Inskeep's Proposal

During the House debate on Snowden's budget speech, Liberal Party member Inskeep made a noteworthy proposal, stating that during the war, the import of luxury goods was banned because the nation's financial resources should be concentrated on important uses. Now, a three-person committee should be organized to study whether it is possible to completely prohibit the import of luxury goods. Inskeep served as Minister of Education and Minister of Commerce in the wartime coalition cabinet and was a leading figure in the shipping industry.

Gandhi Arrives in Marseilles

Enthusiastic Welcome from the Crowd

▲Reuters, Marseilles, 11th - Today, hundreds of people gathered at the pier to await the arrival of the British shipping company's Rajputana, which was carrying Gandhi to London. As the ship docked, Gandhi stood on the deck, wearing only homespun coarse cloth around his waist and a homespun large shawl over his shoulders, despite the damp weather. The crowd cheered thunderously upon seeing him, and Indian students on the shore cheered incessantly, their throats becoming hoarse. Gandhi responded with a hand-to-forehead gesture of respect. When the gangway was lowered, newspaper reporters and photographers rushed forward, and the police could not stop them. Gandhi was trapped in the center of the crowd and asked for forgiveness to retreat temporarily to get some fresh air. It was then decided that reporters who wanted to see him must gather in groups of five or more and could not enter individually. Gandhi is expected to arrive in Folkestone at 1:00 PM tomorrow and then travel to London by car.

Japan Adds Combat Weaponry

▲Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 11th - The Army Aviation Headquarters ordered Mitsubishi Aircraft Company to manufacture a super bomber four years ago, which is expected to be completed this month. The production cost of this new aircraft is 500,000 yuan and is a purely Japanese product. It is equipped with four engines, each with 750 horsepower, and has a cruising speed of 170 kilometers per hour, making it the world's largest fighter.

Continued Discussion on the Wanbaoshan Incident Still Yields No Results

Japanese Consul Suddenly Raises the Twenty-One Demands

Insists on Not Allowing Koreans to Leave the Territory

Zhong Yu Severely Refutes but Remains Adamant

Harbin dispatch: Zhong Yu, special envoy of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, returned to Harbin on August 14 to handle the affairs of the Harbin Municipal Preparatory Office (Zhong also serves as the director) and the negotiation office. He then went to Jilin on August 24 to continue negotiations with the Japanese Consul in Jilin, Ishisa, regarding the Wanbaoshan incident. Because the Japanese Consul refused to allow the Koreans living in the Wanbaoshan area to withdraw from the territory, he went to Liaoning on August 28 to see Zhang Zuoxiang, who was stationed in Shenyang, to seek instructions. He returned to Jilin on August 31 and continued negotiations. However, Ishisa firmly insisted that the Koreans residing in the Zhang Hongbin village in Wanbaoshan have the right to reside in the interior of the eastern provinces, according to Article 21 of the Sino-Japanese Treaty of May 7, 1915, and that this is a vested interest. The text of the treaty clearly states that the Chinese side should not use the Wanbaoshan case as a precondition to demand their withdrawal. Regarding the contract of the Changnong Rice Field Company, the Koreans have the freedom to reside in the local area. It is too late for rice paddies this year, but next year they must continue the original contract and carry out planting. The contract has been approved by the Changchun local government and is valid. During the current period, the Chinese local authorities must do their best to protect the Koreans to prevent them from encountering accidents. Zhong Yu refuted that this case is a local judicial procedure issue, and the validity of the contract should be determined by whether or not it has been formally approved by the government. The intrusion of Koreans into the Chinese interior in Wanbaoshan and the disruption of local order are the preconditions for this case. Therefore, they must first withdraw before the validity of the contract can be discussed. Article 21 was signed by the head of state who did not formally represent China, and the Chinese people have long denied it. It cannot be cited as a basis. Ishisa still refused. After two negotiations, no progress was made. Zhong Yu then went to Liaoning again on September 4 to report to Zhang Zuoxiang. Therefore, local negotiations on this case are temporarily difficult to start. The number of Korean households in the Zhang Hongbin village in Wanbaoshan is still 25, with a population of 60. Although the local farmers refuse to trade with them, the Japanese Consulate in Changchun transports batches of vegetables and food to them to provide relief, and from time to time sends plainclothes police officers to comfort them and investigate the actions of our farmers. Therefore, the Koreans have a talisman and intend to reside there permanently. The ditch near Majiashaokou is still as it was, indicating that this problem is not easy to solve. (6th)

Establishment of the Canal Project Aftermath Committee

Regulations of the Aftermath Committee Amended and Passed

On the 26th of last month, the Jiangbei Canal in Jiangsu Province was impacted by a hurricane, causing breaches in the canal embankment in more than twenty places, large and small. The affected counties along the canal suffered severe disasters. In order to quickly plan for the aftermath, the provincial government specially invited veteran water conservancy experts and canal management experts to organize the Jiangbei Canal Project Aftermath Committee. The inaugural meeting was held in the provincial government conference room yesterday (the 10th). The regulations of the committee were also passed by the provincial government meeting today and are recorded below: (Article 1) The repair of the Jiangbei Canal embankment, the dredging of the outflow channels to the sea, the implementation of industrial disaster relief in Jiangbei, and the management of funds for canal projects shall all be handled by this committee. (Article 2) The committee shall consist of fifteen to nineteen members: A. Five ex-officio members shall be the Chairman of the Provincial Government, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, the Director of the Department of Finance, the Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mining, and the Director of the Department of Construction. B. Ten to fourteen members shall be appointed by the Provincial Government from respected individuals who are familiar with the committee's affairs. (Article 3) The committee shall have one chairman, who shall be elected by the committee. The chairman shall preside over meetings. (Article 4) The committee shall establish an engineering department, with one director, who shall be publicly elected from the committee members to lead it and handle all aftermath engineering affairs. (Article 5) The original personnel of the Canal Works Office shall be under the command of the engineering department. The original engineering personnel of the Water Conservancy Bureau may also be transferred by the engineering department. (Article 6) If the engineering department needs to do so in practice, it may establish engineering offices in designated locations with the approval of the committee. (Article 7) The committee shall establish an industrial disaster relief department, with one director, who shall be publicly elected from the committee members to lead it and handle matters related to using industry to provide disaster relief and assist disaster victims. (Article 8) If the industrial disaster relief department needs to do so in practice, it may establish industrial disaster relief offices in designated locations with the approval of the committee. (Article 9) The committee shall publicly elect three members from the committee members to serve as fund committee members to manage all funds for aftermath engineering and industrial disaster relief. (Article 10) All engineering and industrial disaster relief plans and fund expenditures shall be implemented after being decided by the committee, except for funds that have already been included in the budget. (Article 11) The detailed rules of the committee shall be separately determined and implemented after being decided by the committee. (Article 12) The committee shall establish an evaluation council, which may provide opinions on the implementation methods of various engineering and industrial disaster relief projects at any time for the committee's reference. (Article 13) The members of the evaluation council shall be appointed by the committee from impartial individuals from various counties related to the Jiangbei Canal project. (Article 14) The regulations of the evaluation council shall be separately determined and implemented after being decided by the committee. (Article 15) The committee's budget and the budgets for various engineering and industrial disaster relief projects shall be separately compiled and implemented after being decided by the committee. (Article 16) These regulations shall be decided and promulgated by the provincial government and submitted to the Executive Yuan for record.

Water Disaster Association of Five Counties Asks for Speedy Opening of Company's Water-Blocking Dams

The Zhenjiang, Yancheng, Fudong, and Xinghua Water Disaster Aftermath Association sent a telegram to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, saying: Chairman Ye Junjian, we recently received a telegram from the Dongtai County District Party Department and various legal groups, requesting the provincial government to send troops to assist in opening the Sanmao You River and water-blocking dams of the Dafeng Yuhua and other companies. We then received a telegram on the 30th, stating that Director Zhang and Director Li have been instructed to dispatch teams to assist and notify the Salt Reclamation Company not to obstruct, etc. It was not until late in the day that Senator Zhang, along with Provincial Committee members He Haiqiao and Xu Ji, led a team to Dongtai, which was discussing opening the company's water-blocking dams first and then opening the 800-zhang channel. Suddenly, we heard that Director He telegraphed the province, only mentioning opening the 800-zhang channel, without mentioning opening the company's dams. This contradicted both the provincial government's telegram order and the record of the temporary consultation. It was clearly deceived by the company's false statements. The water is rising, the people are panicking, and the deaths are increasing. The situation is extremely critical. We respectfully plead with you to describe the situation to the provincial government and immediately telegram the various provincial departments to order that the company's water-blocking dams be opened first, followed by the 800-zhang channel to discharge water and save the millions of dying people who are crying for help. Do not be fooled by the company's backers and only open the 800-zhang channel, which the company has been trying to open for many years. This would be like allowing the bladder to function while blocking the throat and internal organs. The water is deep, the disaster is imminent, and the situation is critical. We await your orders with tears and also ask that you forward this to various newspapers for publication to enlist the righteous assistance of all sectors. The Sanmao You River is located within the embankments of the Dafeng and Yuhua companies. Since the dike collapsed, the western water has flowed down, submerging all the counties in the lower reaches. The people of various counties have repeatedly requested that the river and the water-blocking dikes be opened to discharge the water into the sea. At first, they were opened and blocked again, causing public outrage. Now that your government has negotiated with the pacification commissioner to dispatch a team to supervise the opening, we were happy to hear it. However, when your government's committee members executed the order, they deviated from the main issue and first excavated the 800-zhang channel between the Mao You River and Wanggang, intending to discharge the water from Wanggang and still trying to protect the company's dikes. Hundreds of thousands of lives are in the water every day. If we wait for the 800-zhang channel to be opened, we may all perish. The lake water is surging endlessly, and the downstream outlet is so difficult to deal with. Even if the company does not understand righteousness and profit, the government should weigh the importance of the matter. We respectfully implore you to adhere to your original intention, disregard everything, and immediately telegram Director He to quickly open the company's water-blocking dikes, in addition to opening the Sanmao You River, and then open the 800-zhang channel to save the emergency and avoid delays. We await your orders with utmost urgency. The Zhenjiang, Yancheng, Fudong, and Xinghua Water Disaster Aftermath Association bows.

Guo Bingquan's Investigation Report on the Disaster Situation in Xinghua and Vicinity

The breach of the canal caused a great catastrophe. Zhang Zhijiang, the Pacification Commissioner of Jiangsu, attached great importance to this extraordinary disaster. In addition to providing emergency relief in the disaster area, he sent Song Bangrong, his adjutant, to investigate the disaster situation. Recently, he sent Guo Bingquan, an official of the commissioner's office, to Xinghua and vicinity for inspection, as a basis for implementing emergency relief and appealing to the outside world. The following is a transcript of Guo Bingquan's inspection report, to give a glimpse of the disaster situation:

(1) I, in my humble capacity, was ordered to go to Xinghua and Yancheng to investigate the flood disaster. I hired a boat on the second day of this month and went to Shaobo Town. The main hall of the Great King Temple in the town was washed away by the water, and the houses along the embankment were scattered. The breach was being blocked by soldiers of the 25th Route Army in cooperation with the people. I then went to the town's Chamber of Commerce and asked Sun Juru, the person in charge of disaster relief. He said that Shaobo was not far from Zhenyang, and rescue boats were constantly transporting food to the area, so the refugees could be rescued one after another. Even those who did not want to leave had access to relief food, which ensured their survival. I then asked him to help find a boat to Xinghua. However, Shaobo to Xinghua is about 130 miles, and the fields and rivers are indistinguishable, a vast expanse of water. The telegraph has been out of service for a long time. The boatmen either refused because they did not know the way, or replied that the boat was too small. After about three hours, I finally found a boat. Fortunately, the wind was favorable, and I was able to safely cross Shaobo Lake and reach Yangjia Village. The water was deep along the way, measuring about twelve feet. Almost half of the houses in each village had collapsed. A few residents were still nesting in trees, or taking small boats to the high banks of the embankment. I also saw floating coffins drifting by from time to time, the disaster reaching even the remains of the dead. About three miles from the village, a strong northwest wind blew up, and the turbid waves roared. The boat could not stop and drifted with the wind. When we reached a place with many trees, the wind subsided slightly, and we were able to drop anchor. The next morning, after about three hours of sailing, we finally found the original route and crossed Liu'an before we could raise the sail and sail to Fanchuan Town, which is the intersection of Taixian, Jiangdu, and Gaoyou counties. From a distance, the water in the town was about three feet deep. Most of the houses facing the waves had collapsed. There were already two small rescue boats there. We passed the town and followed the Gaotai boundary embankment. The embankment was breached by the water, forming a sawtooth shape. Very few of the telegraph poles along the embankment remained standing. After traveling about five miles along the embankment, the embankment was completely submerged in the water, with only a silver waterline visible. The floodwater flowed eastward, but was blocked by the base of the embankment, causing it to rise and form this silver waterline. At this time, the boat had sailed into the eastern boundary of Gaoyou. The water depth in the rice fields was measured to be about thirteen feet. Soon, we saw a floating corpse, its naked belly swollen like a drum, entangled in the woods. We could tell it was a woman. In the evening, we arrived at Lao Ge Village in Xinghua, passed Wao Village, Shili Pavilion, Balipu, and Wulian, and reached the outside of Xinghua city gate in about ten hours. The water depth in this section was about fourteen feet. Many villagers were living in small boats, guarding their former homes and not leaving. The wilderness outside the south gate of the county was boundless. From the east to Dongtai, from the west to Gaoyou, and from the south to Taixian, the white waves were surging, and there was no end in sight. There were very few villages, resembling an ocean. On the morning of the fourth day, I hired a small boat to enter the city. The water outside the city reached half of the gate, and the houses in the deeper areas were submerged. The water inside the city was also three or four feet deep. The entire city was flooded, except for the county government hall, which was not flooded. When the boat arrived at the county government, it was only eight o'clock. The county magistrate was ill and had not gotten up, and the section chief was also not there. I then went to find Leng Zeng. His family had moved three times from their original residence in Tao Sha Lane to Liu Jia Lane. He said that since the Yun embankment collapsed on August 25, causing the Xinghua disaster, he had taken photographs of the disaster situation and submitted them to Your Excellency. I then went with Leng Zeng to the county government to meet with County Magistrate Hua and inquire about the disaster situation. He replied that since the beginning of summer, there had been torrential rains, which had flooded the fields, accounting for half of the county. On August 3, the Gaoyou Cheluo was opened, and on the 5th, the You Nan Nanguan Dam was also opened. The water rushed down, and the county became a watery country. On the night of August 25, there was a heavy rain and a hurricane. From the six sluices in Shaobo to the Bao Ying Canal Dam, there were more than ten breaches. The county rose more than two feet in a day and night. The low-lying streets inside and outside the city were submerged, and the people in the four rural areas lived in boats. The poor people waited for rescue by clinging to trees, a truly miserable sight. I asked about the areas most severely affected by the disaster. He replied that the entire county was submerged, and it was impossible to distinguish between the severity of the disaster. However, the southeast was higher than the northwest, and fewer people drowned in the higher areas, which could be slightly differentiated. I asked how to provide relief to the refugees. He replied that the county had suffered from insect plagues, droughts, and floods for years, and its finances were extremely strained. The county's 300-plus police force had been in arrears for three months. Even the food in the county government could not be maintained, and there was no power to provide rescue. Fortunately, the provincial government had sent 5,000 yuan for disaster relief, and another 8,000 yuan would be sent soon. The Jiangsu Flood Relief Association would also come to distribute relief. The 5,000 yuan had already been used to purchase flour and distribute it to various districts. A refugee camp had also been set up in the county government, but it was just a drop in the bucket. He hoped that all sectors of society would do their best to help Xinghua, which was on the verge of disaster, so that the people of Xinghua could escape this catastrophe. I asked about the defense situation. He replied that there were occasional bandits stirring, but the county police force, water patrol team, and local defense corps were strictly guarding against them, so they were still able to maintain peace. The various disaster situations could be found in the county's flood disaster investigation report. I asked if he knew about the disaster situation in Yancheng. He replied that the county's telegraph was out of service, and he did not know. However, Yancheng was higher than this county, and it was heard that the early rice had already been harvested, which was thought to be better than this county. I also went with Leng Zeng to the county's Chamber of Commerce. The chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Gu Lunan, described the disaster situation, which was similar to what County Magistrate Hua had said. When asked about the method of receding the water, he replied that it was necessary to block the breaches in Yun Lake and open the Zi Wu Dam (ie, the Dafeng Dam). I said that the Yun Lake breach had been blocked by my superintendent, who had ordered the 25th Route Army to cooperate with the Water Conservancy Bureau and the people. I asked about the necessity of opening Zi Wu. He replied that the Zi Wu Dam was in Dongtai County, about 30 miles from the East China Sea. It was built by Zhang Jian when he developed Nantong. This embankment blocked the floodwater from going to the East China Sea. If this embankment was opened, the floodwater from several counties could be discharged into the East China Sea. However, the Kenmu Company had strong influence. It was heard that there were Japanese shareholders, and they used force to guard the dam and not allow it to be opened. In order to protect their own petty interests, they made the people of seven counties become food for fish and turtles. Please ask the superintendent to find a way to open it. At that time, Shi Zezhi, an inspector from the Department of Civil Affairs, came here from Taixian to observe. He said that the most severely affected area was Xinghua, followed by Gaoyou, Shaobo, Yancheng, Dongtai, and Taixian. When talking about the opening of the Zi Wu Dam, Shi said that he had heard that the Zi Wu Dam was opened on the first day of this month, but then he heard that the Zi Wu Dam was opened and then blocked again. The public deeply hoped that the Zi Wu Dam would be opened, so that there would be a way out. I had already learned that the disaster situation in Yancheng was lighter, and there were few transportation boats. So I entrusted Leng Zeng to submit the disaster situation in Xinghua and other counties to Your Excellency one after another. I then returned to report first. Therefore, I respectfully submit the disaster situation that I have investigated, along with the disaster situation report from the Xinghua County Magistrate, for your information. Investigator, Guo Bingquan.

Distribution of Relief Funds in Jiangsu Province

The Jiangsu Provincial Government recently received a report from the Department of Civil Affairs on the distribution of relief funds. It immediately instructed the department to quickly order officials to claim and distribute the relief funds allocated to the various counties. At the same time, the amount of income and expenditure of the 150,000 yuan of provincial funds previously allocated should be published in the newspapers on a specific date to ensure that everyone knows about it, and a report should be submitted for reference. The following is a transcript of the original report from the Department of Civil Affairs: (According to the instructions No. 6067 of the President's Office, and the telegram from the Relief Committee, the number of deaths and losses from the Gao Shao breach is countless, and it is heartbreaking to talk about it. The government has allocated 130,000 yuan in relief funds to your province. Commissioner Wang Yiting went to Zhen to discuss emergency relief. He sent a telegram to Shanghai the other day, which should have been received. Commissioner Wang Yi Lao should have arrived in Zhen. Please show the tragic state of the disaster at any time, etc. In addition to replying by telegram and ordering the Department of Agriculture and Mining, this order is for the department to comply with and report the disaster situation in each county in detail for verification, and to submit the emergency relief plan discussed for reference. In accordance with this order, after checking this relief fund, the telegram from the Relief Committee was received by the department for the same reason. Commissioner Wang Yiting arrived in Zhen on the 30th, and a relief meeting was held on the same day. Everyone agreed that the disaster was severe and the area was vast. The 130,000 yuan allocated was not enough to distribute. It was decided to borrow from the provincial relief committee to borrow from the provincial relief committee. It was decided to borrow 1 million yuan from the construction public bonds, and sell 200,000 yuan first, and incorporate the 130,000 yuan into the distribution. The remaining 70,000 yuan was allocated to the committee for reserve. Commissioner Wang has gone to Shanghai to negotiate with the bank to handle it. As for the disaster situation in Gao Shao, it is reported that the water has gradually receded, and most of the disaster victims, except for those who have been taken in, have gathered in higher places, waiting for relief urgently. Many streets have not yet recovered, countless houses have been destroyed, and corpses are everywhere, making it difficult to bear to look at. The exact number of losses and deaths will be reported in detail to the department for further reporting. The reply by telegram is on file. In accordance with the previous order, in addition to waiting for the investigation of the disaster situation in each county to be completed, and reporting in detail in another document, the consultation situation and the distribution list will be prepared in advance for reporting, hoping for review and implementation.) Attached is the distribution list of relief funds for each county: Jiangpu 10,000 yuan, Gaoyou 25,000 yuan, Tongshan 10,000 yuan, Xinghua 20,000 yuan, Bao Ying 10,000 yuan, Huai'an 10,000 yuan, Huaiyin 10,000 yuan, Siyang 10,000 yuan, Luhe 10,000 yuan, Dongtai 10,000 yuan, Lianshui 5,000 yuan, Jiangdu 10,000 yuan, Yangzhou 5,000 yuan, Suqian 5,000 yuan, Wanchun 5,000 yuan, Yancheng 10,000 yuan, Funing 10,000 yuan, Taixian 10,000 yuan, Liyang 5,000 yuan, Shuyang 5,000 yuan, Jintan 5,000 yuan, Pixian 3,000 yuan, Xiaoxian 6,000 yuan, Yizheng 3,000 yuan, Rugao 5,000 yuan, Taixing 3,000 yuan, Fengxian 5,000 yuan, Dangshan 3,000 yuan, Suining 3,000 yuan, Yixing 5,000 yuan, Danyang 3,000 yuan, Jurong 2,000 yuan, Donghai 2,000 yuan, Lishui 2,000 yuan, Peixian 2,000 yuan, Ganyu 3,000 yuan, Jiangning 5,000 yuan, Zhenjiang 5,000 yuan.

Han Fuqu Returns to Ji from Bian

Jinan Communication: Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Provincial Government and Director of the Qingxiang Office of Lu and Yu, went to Yu by special train from Ji on the 4th with Jiang Bocheng, Ge Guangting, Peng Shibin, Zhang Honglie, and Zhang Yue, in order to plan the Qingxiang Office of Lu and Yu, and to report to Deputy Commander Zhang in Ping on the meeting with the North China generals on Yan Feng's going abroad and the security situation in North China. They went to Yu to meet with Liu Zhi to discuss everything. Jiang Bocheng then went to Beijing from Bian due to business. Han and his party returned to Lu from Bian at 9:00 p.m. on the 8th after completing their mission. This morning (the 9th) at 8:30 a.m., they passed Xuzhou. At 3:10 p.m., they passed Yanzhou. Gu Liangmin, Commander of the 22nd Division, boarded the train to report on the military and bandit situation. At 6:10 p.m., they passed Tai'an. Ma Hongda, Commander-in-Chief of the 15th Route Army, boarded the train to meet and talk about the interception and suppression of Liu Guitang's troops. At 8:00 p.m., the train passed Zhangxia. All the important party, government, and military officials and Mrs. Han came to the station to welcome them. At 8:45 p.m., the special train arrived at the station. The platform and the roads to the provincial government were heavily guarded. Han got off the train and shook hands with the welcomers one by one. According to reports, during this trip to Bian, he met with Chairman Liu. They had a concrete plan for the Qingxiang Campaign in Lu and Yu, and divided it into several zones for implementation. There were bandits in southern and western Henan, but the rest was still peaceful. When he met Commander Ma in Tai'an, he learned that Liu Guitang's troops had been scattered by the 15th Route Army, and only a small portion had fled into the mountains southeast of Tai'an, which was no longer a problem. Then he took a car with the welcomers to the provincial government (September 9).

Shantou Quarantine Station Negotiates the Recovery of Sovereignty

The British Consul Actually Refused to Accept a Chinese Doctor and Was Humiliated

The Taikoo Steamer Sailed Without Inspection

Shantou Communication: Xu Xiren, the director of the Shantou Quarantine Station, has recently been proceeding smoothly with the recovery of the harbor quarantine rights that have been lost for many years. However, the British Consul stationed in Shantou believes that British ships traveling to the Chinese coast and the British-owned islands in the South Seas account for the first place in Shantou Port. The British Consulate sent the British doctor, Lian Tingli, to take charge of the ship quarantine affairs and collect inspection fees. The income from this item is very large. Therefore, when the former director of the quarantine station, Huo Qizhang, was in office, the British Consul privately signed a secret agreement with Huo. The quarantine station did not ask about the quarantine rights at all. The British Consul only allocated several tens of thousands from the ship fees to the quarantine station for expenses. Recently, Xu Xiren decided to recover the quarantine rights and negotiated with the British Consul many times. There have been no less than ten documents. However, the British Consul refused to return them. The quarantine station then notified the shipping companies that, starting from September 1, the Shantou port quarantine affairs would be inspected and charged by the medical officers dispatched by the station. Anyone who dared to resist would be severely punished. Unexpectedly, the British Consulate also notified the shipping companies at the same time that they must still be inspected and paid by Dr. Lian Henry, otherwise the ships would still have to pay back when they arrived at the British ports. As a result, each went to extremes. On September 1, the Taikoo shipping line's Guangzhou ship sailed to Siam. The medical officer of the quarantine station went on board to check and collect fees. It happened to meet Dr. Lian Henry. The Chinese doctor was actually humiliated. On the 4th, the Taikoo ship Anhui was sailing to Singapore. The British shipowner refused the Chinese medical officer's inspection again. The quarantine station was angry and refused to issue a health certificate. At 5 p.m., the ship obtained the consent of the British Consul and sailed out of the port. The quarantine station believed that the British side deliberately despised our national sovereignty. On the 5th, it sent a telegram to the Guangzhou government to report. The telegram read: (The Shantou Taikoo shipping line first violated the rules and refused to pay the inspection fee, and then on the 4th, the company's Anhui ship sailed without being inspected by my office. Please immediately order the Chao Hai Customs Supervisor to transfer to the Customs Department that all export ships will not be allowed to leave the port without being inspected and issued a health certificate by my office to maintain the quarantine rights. I will submit the rest later.) At the same time, the quarantine station also sent a letter to the British Consul, protesting: (1) The British Consul must make a formal apology, (2) Guarantee that Dr. Lian Henry will not go on board again to overstep his authority to carry out quarantine inspections and that the same incident will not occur again. The results will be reported later. (September 6).

The Qing Municipal Government's Proposal to Fill the Big Port Bay

Use the Reef Mountain Range to Turn the Bay into Land

For the Construction of Warehouses, Docks, and Factories

Qingdao Communication: Since taking office, Qingdao Mayor Hu Ruoyu has established a design committee to develop the city. Since the establishment of the committee, it has made many suggestions for municipal construction. Yuan Daochong, a member of the committee, proposed that there is a concave bay on the northeast side of the breakwater in the city's large port, covering an area of ​​approximately 20,000 acres. Now, due to the gradual rise of sand and the accumulation of tides, the entire area is exposed to the sea surface, forming a small island. It is proposed to fill this bay into land, which can be used for the construction of warehouses, factories, and docks. The committee has submitted the proposal to the city government's municipal meeting, which decided that the three bureaus of Public Works, Port Affairs, and Finance, as well as the Observatory, will form a committee to conduct measurements first, in order to study the method of filling. The original text of the design committee's proposal is recorded below: (It is submitted to suggest filling the concave bay on the northeast side of the breakwater in the big port and organizing a committee to conduct measurements first, hoping for review. According to the proposal of Yuan Daochong, a member of our committee, the northeast side of the breakwater in the city's big port has a coastline that curves into a concave-shaped bay. The southwest corner of this bay is adjacent to the third wharf, the south follows the railway line, encircling to the Sifang station, and the northeast reaches the back of the inner and outer cotton mills. The mountain rocks here enter the sea to form reefs, facing the large reefs on the side of the fifth wharf, forming the gateway to this bay. In recent years, the bay has been filled with sand, and the bottom is completely exposed at low tide, and the reefs on the side of the fifth wharf have been silted into a delta shape, protruding into the sea from the road embankment, with a diameter of about half a kilometer. The opposite bank is the white-filled land of the inner and outer cotton mills, protruding into the sea, accounting for about 2,000 acres. If we use the reef mountain range to build an outer embankment from behind the inner and outer cotton mills, and connect it to the original breakwater, and fill this concave bay into land, the area will be about 20,000 acres. This new land has four uses: (1) The entire area close to the bay can be used for warehouses and open storage areas, (2) The area close to Sifang can be used for large factories and the expansion of the market, (3) The starting point of the big port breakwater is adjacent to the newly filled land, which can be used for adding wharves, (4) Building an embankment from the Haibo River estuary to extend the river channel to reach the newly filled coast, using the tide, which can be used for sailboats to enter and exit. It is proposed that the municipal government select members from the three bureaus of Public Works, Port Affairs, and Finance to conduct preliminary measurements of the sea water depth, tide, soil saturation, the depth of the hard bottom in the bay, and the exact area of ​​the bay, and to jointly investigate the economic needs of all parties with the Railway Bureau, plan the future street layout, and make a plan, and then plan the funding and implement the construction in stages. A map is attached to the meeting. It was submitted to the second meeting on the 12th of this month for discussion. It was agreed that this proposal is of great importance to the future development of the city, and should be forwarded to the President for adoption. However, the original opinion proposed to organize a committee to conduct preliminary measurements. It was decided that in addition to selecting members from the three bureaus of Public Works, Port Affairs, and Finance, personnel from the Observatory should be added to form a joint organization, which would be more perfect. In addition, Committee Member Ding Jingchen temporarily moved that if a branch line could be built from the Jiaoji Railway to Zhan Mountain, more suitable land could be obtained, and a new wharf could be built there. Compared with Committee Member Yuan's proposal to fill the sea, which is more appropriate in terms of economic and factual aspects, it seems necessary to study in detail. This committee believes that Committee Member Ding's motion has a valuable value and should be submitted together for reference. All the reasons for suggesting to fill the concave bay on the northeast side of the breakwater in the big port and organizing a committee to conduct preliminary measurements are hereby submitted together with the original proposal and map of Committee Member Yuan Daochong for your review. (September 8).

Local Communications

Suzhou

Opening of the Appeal Hearing for the Zhuiing Child Murder Case

The appeal case of the child murder in Zhuiing, Songjiang, was heard in the High Court yesterday afternoon. Judge Zhao Zhengtang, Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo, clerks, and other court officials took their seats in the first courtroom. First, Wang Tao was called, and her age and origin were asked. Then, she was asked if she had committed any crimes before, to which she replied that she had not. Next, Xia Aqing, Zhang Mama, and others were asked their ages, origins, and addresses before being dismissed to the side. Wang Tao was asked, "You killed Diqing. What are you dissatisfied with that you are appealing?" She replied, "Diqing was my own son. Of the two sons I bore, the younger one died young. Only Diqing remained. How could I kill him? Do you not think about who would carry my head and see me off after my death?" She was asked, "Was Diqing your own son?" She replied, "Yes. He had already married a woman from the Chen family of Nanqiao as his wife and had a son and a daughter." She was asked, "How many years has your husband been dead?" She replied, "Fifteen years. Diqing was only eight years old at that time." She was asked, "Did you arrange the marriage?" She replied, "Yes." She was asked, "Did he usually do any work?" She replied, "No, he studied at school." She was asked, "Was your son usually well-behaved?" She replied, "People say he was bad, but I relied on him. I cannot say he was bad. I depended on him for my livelihood." She was asked, "How much money did he spend?" She replied, "A lot." She was asked, "How much?" She replied, "He sold several mu of land." She was asked, "What was its value?" She replied, "Two or three hundred dollars." She was asked, "How many people are there in your family in total?" She replied, "Zhang Mama, Wang Yutian, my daughter-in-law, and myself, five people in total." She was asked, "What does Xia Aqing do at your place?" She replied, "He is a mason, helping out at my house." She was asked, "What about Wang Yutian?" She replied, "He is an accountant, my husband's younger brother." She was asked, "Does he live in your house?" She replied, "He comes and goes, it's not fixed. After my husband died, I asked him to come and take care of things." She was asked, "What is your relationship with him?" She replied, "He is my husband's younger brother." She was asked, "Where does he stay when he's at your house?" She replied, "He is in the back, I am in the front." She was asked, "Do you live together?" She replied, "No. You can investigate." She was asked, "How many people sleep in each room?" She replied, "Zhang Mama sleeps with my grandson. My room is at the front." She was asked, "Has Wang Yutian ever lived with you?" She replied, "No." She was asked, "What about eating meals?" She replied, "We sit at the same table, it doesn't matter among family." She was asked, "Zhang Mama said you slept together?" She replied, "Heaven is above, earth is below. My husband has been dead for more than thirty years. If we had slept together, wouldn't we have had children? I am still completely chaste." She was asked, "The neighbors all say you have a relationship with him?" She replied, "They are just talking nonsense." She was asked, "What was the relationship between Diqing and his wife like?" She replied, "Not good, not bad." She was asked, "How exactly did your son die?" She replied, "I was in the front building and rarely went to the back building, so I don't know." She was asked, "When did you first learn of his death?" She replied, "The child had a fever and chills. I went to call him and that's when I found out." She was asked, "How did you see he had died?" She replied, "I cried and fainted, I didn't know." She was asked, "Was he killed by someone, or did he commit suicide?" She replied, "In my confusion, I couldn't tell." She was asked, "Did he die in bed or somewhere else?" She replied, "He hanged himself in the back half of the room." She was asked, "So he hanged himself?" She replied, "Yes." She was asked, "Did anyone come that night?" She replied, "I usually don't pay attention to people coming and going. I don't care about that." She was asked, "Was Xia Aqing at your house?" She replied, "He was outside, not at my house." She was asked, "What about Zhang Mama?" She replied, "She was sleeping with my grandson at my place." She was asked, "Did you ask Mama when he died?" She replied, "I didn't ask." She was asked, "Why did he commit suicide?" She replied, "He was outside, I don't know what he did." She was asked, "What did he do outside?" She replied, "I can't say." She was asked, "Was there an autopsy after his death?" She replied, "I was inside and heard that there was an autopsy." She was asked, "Did the autopsy show that he hanged himself?" She replied, "I was already arrested at that time, how could I know?" She was asked, "You said he hanged himself, but the autopsy showed he was strangled to death, and there were many wounds on his body. He was strangled to death and then made to look like he hanged himself." She replied, "I don't understand." She was asked, "He was your own son, and it happened in your own house. How could you not understand?" She was asked, "Did he have any enemies outside?" She replied, "I don't know about what he did outside." She was asked, "In the Jinshan County Government, you admitted that you, Xia Aqing, and Zhang Mama wanted to get 1,000 dollars from Diqing because you thought he was wasting money, so you killed him." She replied, "They scared me. I never confessed." The judge then brought up the interrogation records from Jinshan County Government. Wang Tao repeatedly denied confessing, saying, "They are falsely accusing me." The judge then said, "Since you confessed, why are you denying it?" She remained silent. She was asked, "So, was it Wang Yutian and Xia Aqing who killed him?" She replied, "Yutian only had this one nephew, how could he kill him?" She was asked, "Xia Aqing confessed that Wang Yutian and you instructed him to kill Diqing." She replied, "That's a false accusation." She was asked, "Why did Wang Yutian flee?" She replied, "He wasn't there at the time. Later, when he came back, people told him to run, so he fled." Next, Xia Aqing was interrogated. He was asked, "What are your reasons for disagreeing and appealing here?" He replied, "I was sipping tea in a teahouse. I was wrongly accused." He was asked, "Were you present when Diqing died?" He replied, "No." He was asked about his occupation. He replied, "Mason. First, I built a house for the Wang family, and then I became their servant." He was asked, "Do you live at their house?" He replied, "Yes, together." He was asked, "For how many years?" He replied, "Six years." He was asked, "How many servants are there in total?" He replied, "Four people." He was asked, "What does Wang Yutian do at their house?" He replied, "Accountant." He was asked, "Where does he live at their house?" He replied, "The back building." He was asked, "Does he sleep in the same room as Wang Tao?" He replied, "I don't go upstairs, I don't know." He was asked, "What was the relationship between the mother and son like?" He replied, "Very good. Was Diqing very wasteful?" He replied, "Yes." He was asked, "What did he use the money for?" He replied, "He liked to play around." He was asked, "How many times did the mother and son quarrel?" He replied, "I don't know." He was asked, "What about with Yutian?" He replied, "Last year, Diqing kicked Yutian out." He was asked, "Did Wang Tao and Yutian have a relationship?" He replied, "I don't know." He was asked, "What about with you?" He replied, "No." The judge then stated that he had already confessed in the Jinshan County Government, so why was he retracting his confession? Xia then confessed that Wang Tao was the mastermind. Next, Zhang Mama was interrogated. According to her testimony, she was holding the grandson when she went to Diqing's room and already saw Diqing's body lying on the bed. She requested to be exonerated. Next, the deceased's wife, Chen Zhaoying, was questioned and requested a settlement. Next, the witnesses Wang Shuzan, Chen Jianquan, Xu Tangrong (clerk of Chongyu Bank), and the young maid were brought in. Prosecutor Zhu argued that the appeals of all parties were without merit. Wang Tao's lawyer, Gu Hongzhang, Xia's lawyer, Shen Yong, and Zhang Mama's lawyer, Yang Jipeng, then presented their arguments. The court announced that the arguments were concluded and the verdict would be announced on the afternoon of the 17th of this month.

Wang Monian and His Wife Committed Suicide by Drowning

Wang Monian, who was just over twenty years old and had previously founded the Thunderbolt News, and his wife, Chen Jinzhen, committed suicide by drowning in the Chusheng Bridge inside Loumen at 8 PM on the 10th because he had been unemployed for a long time and was having difficulty making a living. By the time bystanders noticed and called for help to pull them out, it was too late. The local constable reported the incident to the District Attorney's Office, which dispatched officers to investigate yesterday afternoon (the 11th). While the investigation was ongoing, Wang Chunquan, the father of Wang Monian, arrived and requested that the investigation be waived. He prepared coffins for the burial.

Songjiang

Extension of the Deadline for Payment of Silver Tax by One Month

The First and Second National Tax Collection Offices of this county originally set the deadline for collecting the land tax in silver at August 31st. However, due to slow tax collection, the Finance Bureau submitted a request to the Finance Department, asking for an extension of one month to facilitate tax collection. On the 7th, the Finance Department replied by telegram, approving an extension of one month from the date of the order. A public notice was immediately issued, stating that payment of silver tax would be extended from the 7th of this month to the 7th of October, and late fees would be waived.

The Ding and Wu Families in Qiujing Were Robbed

At around 11 PM last night (the 10th), more than ten robbers speaking a local dialect broke into the home of Ding Zhenyang in Qiujing Township, in the second district of this county. The robbers guarding outside fired shots as a warning. Clothing and other items were stolen. The home of Wu Shunyu, who lived in the same residence, was also affected. The robbers fled with their loot. After the incident, investigators found spent Gao Sheng firecrackers on the ground, indicating that the robbers had used the firecrackers to intimidate the victims.

Arrest of Bandit Leader Yu Guihe

Yu Guihe, who previously served as captain of an anti-smuggling patrol boat in the Suzhou region, had been serving under Taibao Ashu as an alternate battalion commander after leaving his post. He participated in robberies in various cities and towns in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. He recently returned to his hometown, where he was discovered and arrested by Fang, the battalion commander of the Third Battalion of the Security Corps. He confessed to the crimes. He has been handed over to the Pacification Sub-district Headquarters for interrogation.

Qingpu

Unmarried Village Woman Pregnant, Foreman Expelled

Wang Xinyuan, a resident of Pingchao Lou Village in the second district of this county, had no sons. He had only one daughter named Haibao, whom he adopted to continue the family line. He intended to arrange a marriage for his daughter, but her fiancé was unattractive and stubborn. She had an affair with the foreman, Jiang Faquan. Lately, Haibao's belly had grown large, and her mother discovered the secret. She was confined to a room, and the Water Police Team of Jiaoli was notified to arrest Jiang. After someone posted bail, he was expelled from the area.

Qibao Party Affairs Transferred to County Jurisdiction

Qibao's Party affairs were transferred to Shanghai Special Municipality in 1927. The County Rectification Committee felt it was inappropriate for Party and government affairs to be under different jurisdictions. Local Party members requested that Party affairs be transferred back to county control. The County Rectification Committee submitted a request to the Provincial Rectification Committee, which was forwarded to the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters. A representative will be sent soon to take over and return the area to county jurisdiction.

Jiangyin

Student Protest Against Principal Zhang Spreads

More than four hundred students at Nanjing Middle School are protesting against Principal Zhang Zhongyou's mismanagement. On the 8th, the Student Union passed a resolution requesting the Education Department and the School Board to dismiss Principal Zhang. Zhang has left the school and gone to the Education Department to seek instructions. The executive board members decided to request the Principal to return to the school promptly. It was decided that on the 10th the school will organize a student body meeting where Principal Zhang Zhongyou, Accountant Xue Mengyuan, and Teacher Xue Ruchung would address the students. If a concrete solution is not reached by the 15th, all the teachers and staff would collectively resign. It was decided to retain Xue Ruchong and Xue Mengyuan, and they will be requested to remain in their positions. Yesterday morning (the 10th), Chief of Discipline Sun Xuefang, Dean of Studies Xue Xiaosheng, Teacher Liu Minfan and others summoned all the students to a disciplinary talk. Sun Xuefang claimed that this movement was incited by a small number of students, and did not represent the consensus of the majority. He said the movement was illegal. Before he could finish, the students became angry and disgruntled. Gao Qingyue and others spoke in refutation, noting that Director Sun was present during the general assembly and supported the motion. He had witnessed over three hundred and thirty students agreeing to the motion. Regarding the allegation that the motion was illegal, he could explain the eight charges brought against Principal Zhang. The students applauded loudly. The executive committee ordered over three hundred students to form ranks and proceed to the county government to petition County Magistrate Peng. The representatives explained the situation to Magistrate Peng in detail, and Peng offered his earnest advice. He asked the students to follow school rules and attend class. He would travel to Nanjing tomorrow (the 11th) to attend the School Board meeting and address the situation. The students then returned to school and gathered at the playground, where they were asked to sign their names if they supported the dismissal of Principal Zhang, so as to avoid the accusation of being manipulated by a minority. Three hundred and sixty students signed their names. Due to these events, classes were suspended in the morning, and the teachers and staff held another joint meeting. Since classes could not proceed as scheduled, students remained in their classrooms studying. Classes resumed as usual in the afternoon, but the protest against Principal Zhang remained unresolved.

Wuxi

Provincial Office Orders County to Stop Recruiting Soldiers

The county government previously received a letter from Zhang Zheng, commander of the 49th Division of the Army, and the recruiting committee member Qian Baorong came to Wuxi to recruit new soldiers, requesting that the Public Security Bureau provide assistance. Magistrate Chen had previously received a provincial order prohibiting the recruitment of new soldiers in prosperous commercial ports along the Yangtze River. He inquired with the Civil Affairs Office regarding recruitment, and a telegram was received stating that the provincial government had instructed Tongshan and other counties in the former Xu Prefecture to serve as recruiting regions. The coastal areas of the Yangtze River are prosperous commercial ports where recruiting is prohibited. The county has been ordered to adhere to the ordinance and recruit soldiers in the former Xu Prefecture. Magistrate Chen has informed Commander Zhang of the order and directed the Public Security Bureau to persuade Committee Member Qian to cease recruiting. The cocoon industry is opening and prices are being aggressively bidded up. This year's spring cocoon harvest was disastrous, and silk factories are relying on the autumn cocoon harvest. Factories have been making preparations. Due to flooding, only 50% of the autumn cocoons will yield a harvest. The silk markets are sluggish. If prices continue to increase, silk factory profits will decline. Many companies could become stranded. If this is not stopped, factories will fail. The Silk Industry Association has convened an emergency meeting to suppress cocoon prices. The association has chartered many petrol boats, and representatives will be sent to convince the different factories not to aggressively bid.

Provincial Office Orders Strict Collection of Cocoon Industry Business Tax

The Provincial Finance Office has instructed each county to collect the business tax of each industry. The business tax for cocoons had yet to be collected, but this spring's cocoon yields were not good, and traders, because of the temporary nature of the tax, often underreported business numbers or smuggled cocoon bales, or even closed cocoon businesses. Tax revenue was meager, and the public suffered great losses. The autumn cocoon crop is about to come on the market. The county should collect taxes and turn them in at once, in accordance with the regulations. Moreover, at the exit points of cocoon producing counties, the collection agency should assign a temporary investigator to register the number of cocoon bales leaving the country for each cocoon company, so as to verify the business tax with each cocoon company, to prevent smuggling, concealment, and underreporting. This measure has been reported to the Ministry of Finance for record and has been ordered to be implemented by the county offices. Wang Shutang, Director of Wuxi Business Tax Bureau, has instructed the Chamber of Commerce to inform the Silk Industry Association, and will hand in the assessed tax of 1,500 dollars for the summer and autumn seasons.

Changzhou

Investigation Confirms Rape of Six-Year-Old Girl

Zhang Baozhen, a six-year-old adopted daughter of Zhang Sun of Xiaoweitou Village, the ninth district of Wuyi County, was raped by Wang Suode, a seventeen-year-old neighbor. Afterward, Zhang Sun discovered the incident and filed a lawsuit in the County Court. The Prosecutor's Office summoned both parties to court and dispatched an official to examine Baozhen, who confirmed that her hymen was torn, her labia were swollen, and her hymen had been broken, indicating that she had been raped. The prosecutor drafted an indictment and submitted it to the Criminal Court for public trial on the 10th.

Zhenjiang Sends Representatives to Purchase Winter Clothing

Wang Shanbei and Feng Zhixiang, representatives from the Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, arrived in Changzhou on the 10th to purchase 11,000 sets of winter clothing. If they could not find enough clothing, they would travel to Suzhou to purchase additional sets.

Yangzhou

Soy Sauce Industry Association Strives for Sales of Pickles

The Soy Sauce Industry Association of Jiangdu County stated that the Zhenjiang Salt Affairs Anti-Smuggling Team had stopped the sale of Jiangdu pickles at the Xinyuan distribution point on Yinshanmen Street in Zhenjiang, seizing 584 cans of Simei and Su Dachang pickles and fining the shop owner, Zhang Shutang, 120 dollars. Dechang pickles were also seized at the Yiyou store on the riverside. A meeting was held, and representatives Zhao Pinchen and Xu Houqing were elected and introduced by Tang Shou. They proposed to the presidium of the Second Provincial Congress of Jiangsu Province to maintain domestic goods and forward a request to the Zhejiang Transportation Office to punish the team and prohibit it from stopping the transportation and sale of Yangzhou pickle cans and from conducting searches and imposing fines. They also planned to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance's Salt Affairs Bureau to maintain domestic production and prevent harassment of merchants.

Jiaxing

Second District Water Police Return to He after Suppressing Bandits

The Second District Water Police of Jiaxing received a report that several bandit ships were near Miaoqian, on the border of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. District Chief Zhou immediately boarded the Zhiguo warship and led the patrol team to the area. Before reaching Miaoqian, they encountered the bandits, and both sides opened fire. After a fierce battle, the bandits, outnumbered, swam away to escape. Many bandits died in the river. Water police officers Jin Liansheng and Chen Wenbo were killed by gunfire in the battle. Yu Hongsheng, a hostage from Wujiang who was abducted by the bandits on the 24th of August, was rescued. One bandit ship and two guns were seized. The water police who suppressed the bandits have returned to He, and the hostage remains at the district headquarters for his family to reclaim. The Second District Water Police also apprehended bandit kidnappers Yu Zhifa, Yu Bingnan (also known as Yu Yutang), and Wu Yousheng (also known as Wu Yousan) in Dingjia, Jiashan County. Eight Ni family hostages from Hongjiatan were rescued. The three bandits were handed over to the Jiashan County Government for interrogation. With the approval of the Provincial Government via telegraph, the three bandits were executed by firing squad at the scene of the crime yesterday.

Weicheng Factory Workers Petition Party and Government

On the morning of the 10th, over one hundred workers from the Yujia branch of Jiaxing Weicheng Company sent representatives to the County Party Headquarters and the County Government to petition for the implementation of the Factory Law and an increase in wages. Zhu Zhenfan, a standing member of the Party Headquarters, and Gong Shinong, the County Magistrate, gave speeches on the necessity of cooperation between labor and capital. They accepted the petitions and stated that they would separately petition the Provincial Government and the Provincial Party Headquarters for the full implementation of the Factory Law.

Pinghu

The Case of Foreign Bees Harming Rice Crops Remains Unresolved

After the conflict between the Pingyuan Bee Farm in Hanmiao Township and the farmers due to the bees damaging the rice crops, the same incident occurred with the farmers in Xiaoxiao Bridge. Although the County Government issued a notice prohibiting unauthorized relocation, on the one hand, the director of the bee farm was ordered to move out of the area immediately. Sun, the director of the bee farm, argued that bees can pollinate plants, and promoting beekeeping can provide farmers with a secondary source of income and is beneficial, not harmful. Yesterday (the 9th), he moved the beehives to the city to appeal to the County Magistrate and request a solution. However, the farmers strongly opposed it and filed a petition with the County Government, demanding compensation for damages. County Magistrate Wu was in a difficult position, and no suitable solution has been found.

A Notorious Bandit Captured

Since the arrest of Lu Yaosheng, a key member of Taibao Ashu's bandit gang in Pinghu Eastern Township, his followers have scattered. However, his subordinate, the notorious bandit Shen Asi (also known as Long-Legged Asi), who was Lu's vanguard, has been hiding in Wangwan Township in the western part of Zhapu, which belongs to Haiyan County, under the guise of selling smuggled salt. The Pinghu Jin Sinang Bridge Security Corps discovered his hiding place and ordered platoon leader Shen Daosheng to lead over a dozen members, disguised as salt smugglers, and cooperate with County Government bailiff Chen to go to the area. They captured him in a broken house on the afternoon of the 7th.

Shangyu

Bandits Who Robbed Yuyao Fast Boat Confess Accomplices

Fei Zhaosheng (from Sheng County), one of the bandits who robbed a Yuyao fast boat, confessed, after interrogation by the County Government, that Duan, a squad leader from a certain team stationed in the eastern township of this county, and squad leader Zhao were also involved. The county sent a message to the Fifth Battalion in Baiguan, which transferred Duan and Zhao to the county for interrogation on the 8th.

Remnants of Bandit Forces Occupy Dalanshan

The remnants of Shen Yongshou's bandit forces, recently under heavy attack by various units of the Sixth Regiment of the Security Corps, have retreated into Dalanshan, where they are robbing nearby villages to survive.

Soldiers from the Song County Defense Team Extort Money

Chen, a detective from the Song County Defense Team, colluded with a deputy squad leader and soldiers Lou Hongfu, Hu Maochang, and Wang Shouji to extort money from Pan Shuqing in Beihu, Western Township, last month. Pan had been wanted for a previous crime. Wang Xiaoben, Wang Futang, Lian Ruisheng, and others mediated and arranged for Pan to pay 400 dollars to settle the matter. It was also reported that Zhang received over a hundred dollars.

Construction Office Sends Representatives to Test Caojiang Water Power for the Second Time

The Construction Office previously sent representatives to Yu to test the water power of the Caoe River, but the water level was too low. After the typhoon and heavy rain in this county, the water level rose sharply. The Construction Office sent four representatives, including Fan and Ge, to Zhangzhen in southern Yu to conduct tests between the Yue Temple and the Guangfu Temple on the opposite side of the river. The testing site in the middle reaches of the Cao River was 118 meters wide and 5-6 meters deep. The rate and resistance of the water will be precisely calculated upon returning to the province, before the results are released.

Education News

Shanghai Municipal Games Open Today

Opening ceremony at 1 PM at the China Athletic Field

Track and field, soccer, and volleyball competitions will be held today

The much-anticipated Second Shanghai Municipal Games will open at 1 PM today. The area in front of the China Athletic Field on Rue Pere Robert is expected to be crowded with spectators, while the athletes who have been training hard will display their skills on the field and receive cheers from the crowds. The details are as follows:

Promote Civic Sports

Select Representatives for the National Games

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education is holding the Second Municipal Games to promote civic sports, develop citizens' physical fitness, and select representatives for the National Games in 1931.

Overview of Venue Arrangement

Most of the sports events and the opening ceremony will be held at the China Athletic Field. A grand arch stands at the entrance. A canopy has been erected in the center section of the grandstand on the west side of the field, divided into four rooms. The command platform occupies the largest area in the center, with a music platform on the left and the general affairs office and first aid station on the right. A sound system has been set up in front of the command platform. Twelve sheds have been erected outside the running track on the east side of the field for athletes to rest, with four rooms in the south for women and eight rooms in the north for men. The field has been prepared by Field Director Zhou Jiaqi, who has been rolling the track to make it firm and level. The white lines are clear. The soccer, baseball, and tennis courts have also been renovated.
